SELECT [r].[Id], [r].[CreatedAt], [r].[Floor], [r].[Price], [r].[Status], [r].[Title], [r].[UpdatedAt], [r].[UserId], [r0].[Id], [r0].[PhotoUrl], [r0].[RealEstateId], [c].[Id], [c].[ChangeDate], [c].[Description], [c].[RealEstateId]
FROM [RealEstates] AS [r]
LEFT JOIN [RealEstatePhotos] AS [r0] ON [r].[Id] = [r0].[RealEstateId]
